<script language="javascript">
var LayerDir;
function ShowDiv(v, x) {
	LayerDir = v;
	txt = "<table border=0 cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0><tr><td nowrap>";
	txt = txt + x;
	txt = txt + "</td></tr></table>";
	divX_window.innerHTML = txt;
	divX_window.style.top = event.y + document.body.scrollTop;
//	alert(divX_window.top);
	switch(v) {
		case 0: 
			x=event.x + document.body.scrollLeft - divX_window.offsetWidth ; 
			break;
		default:
			x=event.x +document.body.scrollLeft + 20 ; 
	}
	divX_window.style.left = x;
	divX_window.style.display="";	
}
function ShowDiv1(v, x) {
	LayerDir = v;
	txt = "<table border=0 cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0><tr><td nowrap>";
	txt = txt + x;
	txt = txt + "</td></tr></table>";
	divX_window.innerHTML = txt;
	divX_window.style.top = event.y + document.body.scrollTop + 10;
//	alert(divX_window.top);
	switch(v) {
		case 0: 
			x=event.x + document.body.scrollLeft - divX_window.offsetWidth ; 
			break;
		default:
			x=event.x +document.body.scrollLeft + 20 ; 
	}
	divX_window.style.left = x;
	divX_window.style.display="";
	divX_window.style.border="1px; solid #000000";
}

function HideDiv() {
	document.all["divX_window"].style.display = "none";
}
function mouseMove() {
	var x;
	switch(LayerDir) {
		case 0:
			x=event.x + document.body.scrollLeft - 20 - divX_window.offsetWidth ; 
			break;
		default:
			x=event.x +document.body.scrollLeft + 20 ; 
	}
	y=event.y+ document.body.scrollTop + 10;
	moveTo(divX_window, x, y);
}
function moveTo(obj,xL,yL) {
    obj.style.left = xL;
    obj.style.top = yL;
}
//document.onmousemove = mouseMove;
document.write ("<div id='divX_window' style=' display:none; height:20; Z-INDEX: 50; border-style:solid; border-width:1; position:absolute; background-color:#FFFFCC'></div>");

// ##########################################
var OldShowMSGDiv = null; // 혹시 열려진 쪽지보내기버튼이 있는가?
function ShowMSGDiv(objs, x) {
	var txt;
	if (OldShowMSGDiv != null) OldShowMSGDiv.style.display = "none";
}

// 일반유저에게 쪽지보내기
function OpenMsgPop(iduserid) {
	window.open("/etc/member/msgbox.php?iduserid=" + iduserid + "&mode=3", "MSG" , "width=500, height=470, status=yes, scrolls=yes").focus();
}

// 카페회원들에게 쪽지 보내기
function OpenMsgPopToCMember(SciCafeId) {
	window.open("/etc/member/msgbox.php?SciCafeId=" + SciCafeId + "&mode=3", "MSG" , "width=500, height=470, status=yes, scrolls=yes").focus();
}

// 쪽지 수신창 열기
function OpenMsgPopMode1() {
	window.open("/etc/member/msgbox.php?mode=1", "MSG" , "width=500, height=470, status=yes, scrolls=yes").focus();
}

function setCookie( name, value, expiredays ) {
var todayDate = new Date();
todayDate.setDate( todayDate.getDate() + expiredays );
document.cookie = name + "=" + escape( value ) + "; path=/; expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + ";" }

function getCookie( name ) {
var nameOfCookie = name + "=";
var x = 0;

while ( x <= document.cookie.length ) {
var y = (x+nameOfCookie.length);
if ( document.cookie.substring( x, y ) == nameOfCookie ) {
if ( (endOfCookie=document.cookie.indexOf( ";", y )) == -1 )
endOfCookie = document.cookie.length;
return unescape( document.cookie.substring( y, endOfCookie ) ); }
x = document.cookie.indexOf( " ", x ) + 1;
if ( x == 0 )
break; }
return ""; }

function ViewFrame() {
  if (document.all["MyIFrame"].style.display == "") document.all["MyIFrame"].style.display = "none";
  else document.all["MyIFrame"].style.display = "";
}

<script language="javascript">
function TdBgIM(x) {
	$(".cls_Text3_00").css("background-color", "#F6F6F6");
	x.style.backgroundImage = "url(/images/public_v3/background.gif)";
	x.style.backgroundRepeat = "no-repeat";
}
function TdBg(x) {
	$(".cls_Text3_00").css("background-color", "#F6F6F6");
	x.style.backgroundColor = "#e4e3e3";
}

function TdBg2(x) {
//	if (x.style.backgroundColor == "#e4e3e3") $(".cls_Text3_00").css("background-color", "#F6F6F6");
	if (x.style.backgroundColor == "#e4e3e3" || x.style.backgroundColor == "rgb(228, 227, 227)") $(".cls_Text3_00").css("background-color", "#F6F6F6");
	if (x.style.backgroundColor == "#e4e3e3" || x.style.backgroundColor == "rgb(228, 227, 227)") $(".act_cls_Text3_00").css("background-color", "#F6F6F6");
	x.style.backgroundImage = "";
}

</script>

<script language="javascript">
function MakeLogin() {
	_MakeLogin(0); // 개인로그인
}
function MakeLoginL(x) {
	_MakeLoginL(0, x); // 개인로그인
}
function MakeLoginC() {
	_MakeLogin(1); // 기업로그인
}
function MakeLoginCL(x) {
	_MakeLoginL(1, x); // 기업로그인
}

function MakeLogo() {
	_MakeLogo(0); //브릭 로고
}
function UsrAnalysis() {
	_UsrAnalysis(0); //사용자 성향 분석
}
function MakeBView() {
	_MakeBView(0); //BRIC VIEW
}

function _MakeBView(x) {
	var windowWidth = document.body.clientWidth;
	var windowHeight = document.body.clientHeight;
	var windowWidth2;
	var windowHeight2;

	document.body.scrollTop = 0 + 'px';

	MakeBackgroundV();	// 일단 배경부터 생성

	$("#backgroundCenterV").css("display", "block");
	$("#iframePopupV").css("width", "500px");
	$("#iframePopupV").css("height", "300px");
    $("#iframePopupV").attr("src", "/trend/report/view_popup.php"); 

	windowWidth2 = (windowWidth-500)/2;
	windowHeight2 = ($(window).height()-300)/2;
	$("#backgroundCenterV").css("left", windowWidth2 + "px");
	$("#backgroundCenterV").css("top", windowHeight2 + "px");
}

function _UsrAnalysis(x) {
	var windowWidth = document.body.clientWidth;
	var windowHeight = document.body.clientHeight;
	var windowWidth2;
	var windowHeight2;

	document.body.scrollTop = 0 + 'px';

	MakeBackgroundU();	// 일단 배경부터 생성

	$("#backgroundCenterU").css("display", "block");
	$("#iframePopupU").css("width", "636px");
	$("#iframePopupU").css("height", "630px");
    $("#iframePopupU").attr("src", "/about/member/user_analysis.php"); 

	windowWidth2 = (windowWidth-636)/2;
	windowHeight2 = ($(window).height()-650)/2;
	$("#backgroundCenterU").css("left", windowWidth2 + "px");
	$("#backgroundCenterU").css("top", windowHeight2 + "px");
}

function _MakeLogo(x) {
	var windowWidth = document.body.clientWidth;
	var windowHeight = document.body.clientHeight;
	var windowWidth2;
	var windowHeight2;

	MakeBackgroundLo();	// 일단 배경부터 생성

	$("#backgroundCenterLo").css("display", "block");
	//$("#iframePopup").css("width", "330px");
	//$("#iframePopup").css("height", "267px");
	//$("#iframePopup").attr("src", "/login/inner_login.php");
	//windowWidth2 = (windowWidth-330)/2;
	//windowHeight2 = ($(window).height()-267)/2;
	$("#iframePopupLo").css("width", "652px");
	$("#iframePopupLo").css("height", "711px");

	if (x == 1) x = "toComp=Y";
	
	$("#iframePopupLo").attr("src", "/about/logo_popup.php?" + x);

	windowWidth2 = (windowWidth-652)/2;
	windowHeight2 = ($(window).height()-711)/2;
	$("#backgroundCenterLo").css("left", windowWidth2 + "px");
	$("#backgroundCenterLo").css("top", windowHeight2 + "px");
}


function _MakeLogin(x) {
	var windowWidth = document.body.clientWidth;
	var windowHeight = document.body.clientHeight;
	var windowWidth2;
	var windowHeight2;

	document.body.scrollTop = 0 + 'px';

	MakeBackground();	// 일단 배경부터 생성

	$("#backgroundCenter").css("display", "block");
	//$("#iframePopup").css("width", "330px");
	//$("#iframePopup").css("height", "267px");
	//$("#iframePopup").attr("src", "/login/inner_login.php");
	//windowWidth2 = (windowWidth-330)/2;
	//windowHeight2 = ($(window).height()-267)/2;
	$("#iframePopup").css("width", "340px");
	$("#iframePopup").css("height", "285px");

	if (x == 1) x = "toComp=Y";
	
	$("#iframePopup").attr("src", "/login/inner_login.php?" + x);

	windowWidth2 = (windowWidth-340)/2;
	windowHeight2 = ($(window).height()-285)/2;
	$("#backgroundCenter").css("left", windowWidth2 + "px");
	$("#backgroundCenter").css("top", windowHeight2 + "px");
}
function _MakeLoginL(x, L) {
	var windowWidth = document.body.clientWidth;
	var windowHeight = document.body.clientHeight;
	var windowWidth2;
	var windowHeight2;

	document.body.scrollTop = 0 + 'px';

	MakeBackground();	// 일단 배경부터 생성

	$("#backgroundCenter").css("display", "block");
	//$("#iframePopup").css("width", "330px");
	//$("#iframePopup").css("height", "267px");
	//$("#iframePopup").attr("src", "/login/inner_login.php");
	//windowWidth2 = (windowWidth-330)/2;
	//windowHeight2 = ($(window).height()-267)/2;
	$("#iframePopup").css("width", "340px");
	$("#iframePopup").css("height", "285px");

	if (x == 1) x = "toComp=Y";
	x = x + "&dummy=1&BackLink=" + L;
	
	$("#iframePopup").attr("src", "/login/inner_login.php?" + x);

	windowWidth2 = (windowWidth-340)/2;
	windowHeight2 = ($(window).height()-285)/2;
	$("#backgroundCenter").css("left", windowWidth2 + "px");
	$("#backgroundCenter").css("top", windowHeight2 + "px");
}


// 이상호 사용자정의
function MakeBackground() {
	var windowWidth = document.body.clientWidth;
	var windowHeight2 = document.body.scrollHeight;
	if (windowHeight2 < document.body.clientHeight) {
		windowHeight2 = document.body.clientHeight;
	}

	$("#backgroundLayer").css({
		"position": "absolute",
		"top": 0,
		"left": 0,
		"height": windowHeight2,
		"width": windowWidth,
		"z-index": 98
	});

	$("#backgroundLayer").css({
		"opacity": "0.7"
	});
	$("#backgroundLayer").fadeIn("slow");
}
function MakeBackgroundLo() {
	var windowWidth = document.body.clientWidth;
	var windowHeight2 = document.body.scrollHeight;
	if (windowHeight2 < document.body.clientHeight) {
		windowHeight2 = document.body.clientHeight;
	}
	$("#backgroundLayerLo").css({
		"position": "absolute",
		"top": 0,
		"left": 0,
		"height": windowHeight2,
		"width": windowWidth,
		"z-index": 98
	});

	$("#backgroundLayerLo").css({
		"opacity": "0.7"
	});
	$("#backgroundLayerLo").fadeIn("slow");
}
function MakeBackgroundU() {
	var windowWidth = document.body.clientWidth;
	var windowHeight3 = document.body.scrollHeight;
	if (windowHeight3 < document.body.clientHeight) {
		windowHeight3 = document.body.clientHeight;
	}

	$("#backgroundLayerU").css({
		"position": "absolute",
		"top": 0,
		"left": 0,
		"height": windowHeight3,
		"width": windowWidth,
		"z-index": 98
	});

	$("#backgroundLayerU").css({
		"opacity": "0.7"
	});
	$("#backgroundLayerU").fadeIn("slow");
}
function MakeBackgroundV() {
	var windowWidth = document.body.clientWidth;
	var windowHeight3 = document.body.scrollHeight;
	if (windowHeight3 < document.body.clientHeight) {
		windowHeight3 = document.body.clientHeight;
	}

	$("#backgroundLayerV").css({
		"position": "absolute",
		"top": 0,
		"left": 0,
		"height": windowHeight3,
		"width": windowWidth,
		"z-index": 98
	});

	$("#backgroundLayerV").css({
		"opacity": "0.7"
	});
	$("#backgroundLayerV").fadeIn("slow");
}

// 이상호 사용자정의
function ClearBackground() {
	//
	$("#backgroundCenter").css("display", "none"); // iframe 레이어 제거
	$("#backgroundLayer").fadeOut("slow");
}
function ClearBackground2() {
	ClearBackground(); // 배경레이어 제거
}
function ClearBackgroundLo() {
	//
	$("#backgroundCenterLo").css("display", "none"); // iframe 레이어 제거
	$("#backgroundLayerLo").fadeOut("slow");
}
function ClearBackground2Lo() {
	ClearBackgroundLo(); // 배경레이어 제거
}
function ClearBackgroundU() {
	//
	$("#backgroundCenterU").css("display", "none"); // iframe 레이어 제거
	$("#backgroundLayerU").fadeOut("slow");
}
function ClearBackground2U() {
	ClearBackgroundU(); // 배경레이어 제거
}
function ClearBackgroundV() {
	//
	$("#backgroundCenterV").css("display", "none"); // iframe 레이어 제거
	$("#backgroundLayerV").fadeOut("slow");
}
function ClearBackground2V() {
	ClearBackgroundV(); // 배경레이어 제거
}

<script language="javascript">
function SearchTopF() {
	if (document.searchForm.kwd.value.trim().length == "") {
		alert("검색어를 입력하세요.");
		return false;
	}
}
function SearchTotal(f) {
	f.category.value = "TOTAL";
	if (f.kwd.value.trim().length == "")
	{
		alert("검색어를 입력하세요.");
		return false;
	} 
	else
    {	
	    f.submit();
	}
}

<div style="position:relative; left:0px; TOP:-116px; WIDTH:83px; Z-INDEX:1; padding-top:5px;" id="divAd_Nums">
<script language="javascript">
var adDiv = new Array();
adDiv[0] = "2";
adDiv[1] = "1";
// 최초 광고 보임
document.getElementById("divAd_" + adDiv[0]).style.display="block";

var goSideAd = 1;
var goSleep = 0;
var curSideAdIdx = 1;
var LastAd = 0;
function RotateSideAd() {
	var k;
	if (goSideAd == 1) {
		// 측면광고 계속 하라는 플래그일때...

		// 화면 중간에 Loading 이라는 레이어가 있을지 모르지만 그것을 일시적으로 감춤
		document.getElementById("divAd_Sleep").style.display = "none";
		
		// 현재 순번에 해당하는 배열에서 광고번호를 뽑아 출력.
		for(k=1;k <= 2;k++) {
			if (k == curSideAdIdx) {
				document.getElementById("divAd_" + adDiv[k - 1]).style.display="block";
				//document.getElementById("num_" + k).src="/images/public/hot" + k + ".gif";
				document.getElementById("num_" + k).src="http://gene.postech.ac.kr/images/public/hot" + k + ".gif";
			}
			else 
			{
				document.getElementById("divAd_" + adDiv[k - 1]).style.display="none";
				//document.getElementById("num_" + k).src="/images/public/ghot" + k + ".gif";
				document.getElementById("num_" + k).src="http://gene.postech.ac.kr/images/public/ghot" + k + ".gif";
			}

		}
		curSideAdIdx++; // 만약 배열인덱스가 전체 크기를 초과하면 1부터 다시
		if (curSideAdIdx > 2) curSideAdIdx = 1;
		
		// 이번에 광고가 나왔으므로 5초뒤 잠자기.
		if (2 > 1) setTimeout("setSleepAd()", 20000);  //배너 1개일 경우 loading 안되게 수정 2011.8.8
	}
	else
	{
		// 광고 중지.
/*
		// 혹시 Loading 에 걸려있지 않은지 확인.
		if (document.getElementById("divAd_Sleep").style.display == "block") {
			document.getElementById("divAd_Sleep").style.display = "none";
			
			// 다음 광고를 한컷 살린다.
			LastAd = 1;
			RotateSideAd();
		}
*/
	}
}
function setSleepAd() {
	if (goSideAd == 1) {
		// 현재 화면에 나온 광고 레이어의 크기를 구한다.
		document.getElementById("divAd_Sleep").style.display = "block";
	
		for(k=1;k <= 2;k++) {
			document.getElementById("divAd_" + adDiv[k - 1]).style.display="none";
		}
		
		// 모든 레이어를 숨겼다. 그리고 0.5초뒤 다시 광고 시작
		setTimeout("RotateSideAd()", 500);
	}
}
$(document).ready(function() {
	RotateSideAd(); // 광고 돌리기 시작
});

// 해당하는 번호가 눌렸을때...
function GoAd(x) {
	document.getElementById("divAd_1").style.display="none";
	document.getElementById("num_1").src="/images/public/ghot1.gif";
	document.getElementById("divAd_2").style.display="none";
	document.getElementById("num_2").src="/images/public/ghot2.gif";
	// Loading 레이어 죽이기.
	document.getElementById("divAd_Sleep").style.display = "none";

	// 해당 광고만 켜기
	document.getElementById("divAd_" + adDiv[x - 1]).style.display="block";;
	document.getElementById("num_" + x).src="/images/public/hot" + x + ".gif";
	goSideAd = 0;
}
</script>
</div>

<script language="javascript">
function ViewPopm() {
	if (document.getElementById("layerPopm").style.display == 'block') {
		document.getElementById("layerPopm").style.display='none';
	}
	else
	{
		document.getElementById("layerPopm").style.display='block';
	}
}
function ClosePopm() {
      document.getElementById("layerPopm").style.display='none';
}

<script language="javascript">
function ShowGuard(x) {
	document.getElementById("clear_Index").innerHTML = x;

	document.getElementById("clear_Left").style.display = "block";
	document.getElementById("clear_Top").style.display = "block";
	document.getElementById("clear_Right").style.display = "block";
}
function HideGuard() {
	var x = document.getElementById("clear_Index").innerHTML;

	document.getElementById("clear_Left").style.display = "none";
	document.getElementById("clear_Top").style.display = "none";
	document.getElementById("clear_Right").style.display = "none";
	
	TSwap(1, x);
}
</script>

<script language="javascript">
function BscPopup() {
	var windowWidth = document.body.clientWidth;
	var windowHeight = document.body.clientHeight;
	var windowWidth2;
	var windowHeight2;

	document.body.scrollTop = 0 + 'px'; 

	MakeBackground();	// 일단 배경부터 생성

	$("#backgroundCenter").css("display", "block");
	$("#iframePopup").css("width", "506px");
	$("#iframePopup").css("height", "400px");
	$("#iframePopup").attr("src", "/bioschedule/popup_Biosc.php"); 
	windowWidth2 = (windowWidth-506)/2;
	windowHeight2 = ($(window).height()-400)/2;
	$("#backgroundCenter").css("left", windowWidth2 + "px");
	$("#backgroundCenter").css("top", windowHeight2 + "px");
}
</script>

function BiojobPopup(types) {

	var windowHeight = document.body.clientHeight;

	windowHeight2 = ($(window).height()-208)/2;
	$("#backgroundCenter").css("left", windowWidth2 + "px");
	$("#backgroundCenter").css("top", windowHeight2 + "px");
}
</script>

function ISoriPopup() {
	var windowWidth = document.body.clientWidth;
	var windowHeight = document.body.clientHeight;
	var windowWidth2;
	var windowHeight2;

	document.body.scrollTop = 0 + 'px'; 

	MakeBackground();	// 일단 배경부터 생성

	$("#backgroundCenter").css("display", "block");
	$("#iframePopup").css("width", "660px");
 
	$("#iframePopup").css("height", "340px");
	$("#iframePopup").attr("src", "/community/isori_popup.php");
	windowWidth2 = (windowWidth-561)/2;
	windowHeight2 = ($(window).height()-508)/2;
	$("#backgroundCenter").css("left", windowWidth2 + "px");
	$("#backgroundCenter").css("top", windowHeight2 + "px");
}

<script language="javascript">
function TSwap(x, y) {

	var i = 0;
	switch(x) {
		case 0:
			$("#div_cover_topmenu").css("display", "block");
			// 이미지 변경
			for(i=0;i < 10;i++) {
				if (i == y) {
					document.getElementById("div_tmenu0" + i).style.display="none";
					document.getElementById("div_tmenu0" + i + "s").style.display="block";
				}
				else
				{
					// 메뉴들을 정상화
					document.getElementById("div_tmenu0" + i).style.display="block";
					document.getElementById("div_tmenu0" + i + "s").style.display="none";
				}
			}
			ShowGuard(y);
			break;
		case 1:
			// 이미지 복귀
			document.getElementById("div_tmenu0" + y).style.display="block";
			document.getElementById("div_tmenu0" + y + "s").style.display="none";
	}
}
function ShowAllMenu() {
	var i = 0;
	
	$("#div_topMenu3").css("display", "block");
	for(i=0;i < 10;i++) {
		// 메뉴들을 정상화
		document.getElementById("div_tmenu0" + i).style.display="block";
		document.getElementById("div_tmenu0" + i + "s").style.display="none";
	}

	$("#allBtn").css("left", (parseInt($("#div_topMenu_All_Border").css("width")) * 1 - 50 + 2) + "px");
	$("#allBtn").css("top", (parseInt($("#div_topMenu_All_Border").css("height")) * 1 - 20 + 6) + "px");

}
function HideAllMenu() {
	$("#div_topMenu3").css("display", "none");
}
</script>
</div>

<script language="javascript">
function HideKeyText(x) {
	var form = document.searchForm;
	
	if (form.kwd.value == x) {
		form.kwd.value = "";
	}
}
</script>

<script language="javascript">
// HTML5 가 아닌 페이지에서 오류가 나는것을 방지. 상단 통합검색창
// 단 about 용은 top_about.php 에서 처리
$(window).resize(function() {
	SearchPosition();
});

function SearchPosition() {
	var ww = $(window).width();
	var ww2;
	ww = ww - 944;
	ww = ww/2;
	ww = ww + 712 - 10;
	ww2 = ww - 130;
	$("#div_Search2").css("left", ww + "px");
	$("#div_Search2").css("top", "35px");
	$("#div_Scroll").css("left", ww2 + "px");
	$("#div_Scroll").css("top", "50px");
}
SearchPosition();
</script>

<script language="javascript">
var old_redLeft = 0;
function showLeftContents(x) {
	// 레이어 숨기기	
	$("#div_redLeft_1_" + old_redLeft).css("display", "none");
	$("#redLeft" + old_redLeft).removeClass("cls_redLeft_Hover");
	$("#redLeft" + old_redLeft).removeClass("cls_redLeft_Hover1");
	$("#redLeft" + old_redLeft).removeClass("cls_redLeft_Hover2");

    if (6 != x) {
	    $("#redLeft" + old_redLeft).addClass("cls_redLeft"); 
	}

	for(i=0;i < 11;i++) { 
		if (i == x) {
			$("#div_redLeft_1_" + x).css("display", "block");
		}
		else
		{
			$("#div_redLeft_1_" + i).css("display", "none");
		}
	}

    if (6 != x) {
	    $("#redLeft" + old_redLeft).addClass("cls_redLeft"); 
	}
	$("#redLeft" + x).removeClass("cls_redLeft");

	$("#redLeft" + x).addClass("cls_redLeft_Hover");
	old_redLeft = x;
}
function showLeftContents1(x) {
	// 레이어 숨기기	
	$("#div_redLeft_1_" + old_redLeft).css("display", "none");
	$("#redLeft" + old_redLeft).removeClass("cls_redLeft_Hover");
	$("#redLeft" + old_redLeft).removeClass("cls_redLeft_Hover1");
	$("#redLeft" + old_redLeft).removeClass("cls_redLeft_Hover2");
	$("#redLeft" + old_redLeft).addClass("cls_redLeft");

	//$("#redLeft" + x).removeClass("cls_redLeft");

	for(i=0;i < 11;i++) { 
		if (i == x) {
			$("#div_redLeft_1_" + x).css("display", "block");
		}
		else
		{
			$("#div_redLeft_1_" + i).css("display", "none");
		}
	}

    $("#redLeft" + x).removeClass("cls_redLeft");

	$("#redLeft" + x).addClass("cls_redLeft_Hover1");
	old_redLeft = x;
}
function showLeftContents2(x) {
	// 레이어 숨기기	
	$("#div_redLeft_1_" + old_redLeft).css("display", "none");
	$("#redLeft" + old_redLeft).removeClass("cls_redLeft_Hover");
	$("#redLeft" + old_redLeft).removeClass("cls_redLeft_Hover1");
	$("#redLeft" + old_redLeft).removeClass("cls_redLeft_Hover2");
	$("#redLeft" + old_redLeft).addClass("cls_redLeft");

	if(x == 6) {
	    //$("#redLeft" + x).removeClass("cls_redLeft");
	}


	for(i=0;i < 11;i++) {
		if (i == x) {
			$("#div_redLeft_1_" + x).css("display", "block");
		}
		else
		{
			$("#div_redLeft_1_" + i).css("display", "none");
		}
	}


	if(x == 6) {
	    //$("#redLeft" + x).removeClass("cls_redLeft");
	}
	$("#redLeft" + x).addClass("cls_redLeft_Hover2");
	old_redLeft = x;
}
</script>

<script language="javascript">

function goRightV() { 
   var r4Lines = 4;
   var CurLine = document.getElementById("P_RANDOM").innerHTML;
   var temp = CurLine;

   if (temp == 1) temp = 2;
   else if (temp == 2) temp = 3;
   else if (temp == 3) temp = 4;
   else if (temp == 4) temp = 5;
   else if (temp == 5) temp = 6;

   if (temp > r4Lines) {
		temp = 1;
   }

	$("#tr_ip_tr" + CurLine).css("display", "none");
    $("#tr_ip_tr" + temp).css("display", "block");

    document.getElementById("P_RANDOM").innerHTML = temp;
}

function goLeftV() { 
   var r4Lines = 4;
   var CurLine = document.getElementById("P_RANDOM").innerHTML;
   var temp = CurLine;

   if (temp == 1) temp = 0;
   else if (temp == 2) temp = 1;
   else if (temp == 3) temp = 2;
   else if (temp == 4) temp = 3;
   else if (temp == 5) temp = 4;
   else if (temp == 6) temp = 5;
  
   if (temp < 1) { 
		temp = r4Lines;
   }


	$("#tr_ip_tr" + (CurLine)).css("display", "none");
	$("#tr_ip_tr" + temp).css("display", "block");

	document.getElementById("P_RANDOM").innerHTML = temp;
}
</script>

<script language="javascript">
function left5On(x) {
	var i;
	
	for(i=1;i <= 4;i++) {
		if (i == x) {
			$("#left5_td" + i).addClass("left5_Active");
			$("#left5_td" + i).removeClass("left5_DeActive");
			
			$("#tr_biojob" + i).css("display", "block");
		}
		else
		{
			$("#left5_td" + i).addClass("left5_DeActive");
			$("#left5_td" + i).removeClass("left5_Active");

			$("#tr_biojob" + i).css("display", "none");
		}
	}
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var rTabs = 2;
function rTabOn(x) {
	var i = 0;
	for(i=1;i <= rTabs;i++) {
		if (i == x) {
			$("#td_rt" + i).removeClass("right1_td_type1").addClass("right1_td_type2");
			$("#right_inner" + i).css("display", "");
		}
		else
		{
			$("#td_rt" + i).removeClass("right1_td_type2").addClass("right1_td_type1");
			$("#right_inner" + i).css("display", "none");
		}
	}
}
rTabOn(2);
</script>				<meta http-equiv="Content-Type" content="text/html; charset=euc-kr" />

<script language="javascript">
var r4Lines = 4;
var r4CurLine = 1;

function goR4Rightv() {
	var temp = r4CurLine;
	if (temp + 1 > r4Lines) {
		temp = 1;
	}
	else temp = temp + 1;

	$("#tr_r4_tr" + r4CurLine).css("display", "none");

	r4CurLine = temp;
	$("#tr_r4_tr" + temp).css("display", "block");
	temp++;
}

function goR4Leftv() {
	var temp = r4CurLine;
	if (temp - 1 < 1) {
		temp = r4Lines;
	}
	else temp = temp - 1;

	$("#tr_r4_tr" + (r4CurLine)).css("display", "none");

	r4CurLine = temp;
	$("#tr_r4_tr" + temp).css("display", "block");
	temp--;
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var rTabs3 = 6;
function rTabOn3(x) {
	var i = 0;
	for(i=1;i <= rTabs3;i++) {
		if (i == x) {
			$("#right3_tab" + i).removeClass("tabs").addClass("tabs2");
			$("#tbl_right3_2_" + i).css("display", "block");
		}
		else
		{
			$("#right3_tab" + i).removeClass("tabs2").addClass("tabs");
			$("#tbl_right3_2_" + i).css("display", "none");
		}
		if (x == 1) {
		}
		else
		{
			$("#td_612").css("display", "none");
		}
	}
}

function rTabOn41(x) {
	$("#right3_tab" + x).removeClass("tabs4").addClass("tabs");

}
function Show612() {
	$("#div_612_open").css("display", "none");
	$("#div_612_close").css("display", "block");
	$(".cls_list612_12").css("display", "block");
	MyIFrame.document.location = "/main/_setcookie.php?td612=show";
}
function Hide612() {
	$("#div_612_open").css("display", "block");
	$("#div_612_close").css("display", "none");
	$(".cls_list612_12").css("display", "none");
	MyIFrame.document.location = "/main/_setcookie.php?td612=hide";
}

<script language="javascript">
function right5On(x) {
	var i;
	
	for(i=1;i <= 2;i++) {
		if (i == x) {
			$("#right5_td" + i).addClass("right5_Active");
			$("#right5_td" + i).removeClass("right5_DeActive");
			
			$("#tr_biomarket" + i).css("display", "block");
		}
		else
		{
			$("#right5_td" + i).addClass("right5_DeActive");
			$("#right5_td" + i).removeClass("right5_Active");

			$("#tr_biomarket" + i).css("display", "none");
		}
	}
}
</script>

<script language="javascript">
var r5PELines = 1;
var r5PECurLine = 1;

function goR5PERightv() {
	var petemp = r5PECurLine;
	if (petemp + 1 > r5PELines) {
		petemp = 1;
	}
	else petemp = petemp + 1;

	$("#tr_r5PE_tr" + r5PECurLine).css("display", "none");

	r5PECurLine = petemp;
	$("#tr_r5PE_tr" + petemp).css("display", "block");
	petemp++;
}

function goR5PELeftv() {
	var petemp = r5PECurLine;
	if (petemp - 1 < 1) {
		petemp = r5PELines;
	}
	else petemp = petemp - 1;

	$("#tr_r5PE_tr" + (r5PECurLine)).css("display", "none");

	r5PECurLine = petemp;
	$("#tr_r5PE_tr" + petemp).css("display", "block");
	petemp--;
}
</script>

     </td>

<script language="javascript">
function goR5Left() { 
   var r5Lines = 6;
   var r5CurLine = document.getElementById("R_RANDOM").innerHTML;
   var temp = r5CurLine;
   var r5CurLine1, r5CurLine2, r5CurLine1, temp1, temp2, temp3;

   //alert(r5CurLine);

   if (r5CurLine == 1) r5CurLine1 = 1;
   else if (r5CurLine == 2) r5CurLine1 = 4;
   else if (r5CurLine == 3) r5CurLine1 = 7;
   else if (r5CurLine == 4) r5CurLine1 = 10;
   else if (r5CurLine == 5) r5CurLine1 = 13;
   else if (r5CurLine == 6) r5CurLine1 = 16;

   //alert("r5CurLine1");
   //alert(r5CurLine1);

   if (r5CurLine1 + 1 > r5Lines ) { 
	   r5CurLine2 = 1;
	   r5CurLine3 = 2;
   }
   else 
   { 
	   r5CurLine2 = r5CurLine1 + 1;
       if (r5CurLine1 + 2 > r5Lines ) { 
	       r5CurLine3 = 1;
       }
	   else 
	   { 
		   r5CurLine3 = r5CurLine1 + 2;
	   }
   }

   //alert(r5CurLine2);
   //alert(r5CurLine3);

   //alert("temp");
   //alert(temp);

   if (temp == 1) temp1 = r5Lines;
   else if (temp == 2) temp1 = 3;
   else if (temp == 3) temp1 = 6;
   else if (temp == 4) temp1 = 9;
   else if (temp == 5) temp1 = 12;
   else if (temp == 6) temp1 = 15;

   if (temp1 - 1 < 1) { 
	   temp2 = r5Lines;
	   temp3 = r5Lines - 1;
   }
   else 
   { 
       temp2 = temp1 - 1;
       if (temp1 - 2 < 0 ) { 
		  temp3 = r5Lines;
       }
	   else 
	   { 
		  temp3 = temp1 - 2;
	   }
   }

   //alert(temp1);
   //alert(temp2);
   //alert(temp3);

   $("#tr_r5_tr" + r5CurLine1).css("display", "none");
   $("#tr_r5_tr" + r5CurLine2).css("display", "none");
   $("#tr_r5_tr" + r5CurLine3).css("display", "none");

   $("#tr_r5_tr" + temp1).css("display", "block");
   $("#tr_r5_tr" + temp2).css("display", "block");
   $("#tr_r5_tr" + temp3).css("display", "block");


   if (temp3 < 4) temp = 1;
   else if (temp3 < 7) temp = 2;
   else if (temp3 < 10) temp = 3;
   else if (temp3 < 13) temp = 4;
   else if (temp3 < 16) temp = 5;
   else if (temp3 < 19) temp = 6;

   document.getElementById("R_RANDOM").innerHTML = temp;
}

function goR5Right() { 
   var r5Lines = 6;
   var r5CurLine = document.getElementById("R_RANDOM").innerHTML;
   var temp = r5CurLine;
   var r5CurLine1, r5CurLine2, r5CurLine1, temp1, temp2, temp3;

   //alert(r5CurLine);

   if (r5CurLine == 1) r5CurLine1 = 1;
   else if (r5CurLine == 2) r5CurLine1 = 4;
   else if (r5CurLine == 3) r5CurLine1 = 7;
   else if (r5CurLine == 4) r5CurLine1 = 10;
   else if (r5CurLine == 5) r5CurLine1 = 13;
   else if (r5CurLine == 6) r5CurLine1 = 16;

   //alert("r5CurLine1");
   //alert(r5CurLine1);

   if (r5CurLine1 + 1 > r5Lines ) { 
	   r5CurLine2 = 1;
	   r5CurLine3 = 2;
   }
   else 
   { 
	   r5CurLine2 = r5CurLine1 + 1;
       if (r5CurLine1 + 2 > r5Lines ) { 
	       r5CurLine3 = 1;
       }
	   else 
	   { 
		   r5CurLine3 = r5CurLine1 + 2;
	   }
   }

   //alert(r5CurLine2);
   //alert(r5CurLine3);

   //alert("temp");
   //alert(temp);

   if (temp == 1) temp1 = 4;
   else if (temp == 2) temp1 = 7;
   else if (temp == 3) temp1 = 10;
   else if (temp == 4) temp1 = 13;
   else if (temp == 5) temp1 = 16;
   else if (temp == 6) temp1 = 17;

   if(temp1 > r5Lines) temp1 = 1;

   if (temp1 + 1 > r5Lines ) { 
	   temp2 = 1;
	   temp3 = 2;
   }
   else 
   { 
       temp2 = temp1 + 1;
       if (temp1 + 2 > r5Lines ) { 
		  temp3 = 1;
       }
	   else 
	   { 
		  temp3 = temp1 + 2;
	   }
   }

   //alert(temp1);
   //alert(temp2);
   //alert(temp3);

   $("#tr_r5_tr" + r5CurLine1).css("display", "none");
   $("#tr_r5_tr" + r5CurLine2).css("display", "none");
   $("#tr_r5_tr" + r5CurLine3).css("display", "none");

   $("#tr_r5_tr" + temp1).css("display", "block");
   $("#tr_r5_tr" + temp2).css("display", "block");
   $("#tr_r5_tr" + temp3).css("display", "block");

   if (temp3 < 4) temp = 1;
   else if (temp3 < 7) temp = 2;
   else if (temp3 < 10) temp = 3;
   else if (temp3 < 13) temp = 4;
   else if (temp3 < 16) temp = 5;
   else if (temp3 < 19) temp = 6;

   document.getElementById("R_RANDOM").innerHTML = temp;
}

</script>
